18-20 Point Standard Decklists
==============================



 Posted in [PRO TOUR MAGIC ORIGINS](/en/events/coverage/ptori)
 on August 2, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast











 A total of 37 players earned 18-20 points from their Standard rounds at Pro Tour *Magic Origins*, with 30 of those players finishing with 18 points (6-3) and the other seven grabbing an extra point to finish with 19 (6-2-1).





---


**The following players finished with 19 points (6-2-1) in Standard:**









#### Pierre Dagen


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-e6665643b81bdd2f25dbda5868508a1c.txt?n=Pierre%20Dagen)
